raphael_move_forward:

$0F/B4AB 20 AF B1    JSR $B1AF  [$00:B1AF]   ;
$0F/B4AE AD 6C 10    LDA $106C  [$00:106C]   ; \
$0F/B4B1 10 07       BPL $07    [$B4BA]      ;  | attempts to correct
$0F/B4B3 AD 5C 10    LDA $105C  [$00:105C]   ;  | Y value if >= $43
$0F/B4B6 C9 43       CMP #$43                ;  |
$0F/B4B8 90 12       BCC $12    [$B4CC]      ;  | applies a simple gravity
$0F/B4BA AD 5C 10    LDA $105C  [$00:105C]   ;  | decrementing Y velocity
$0F/B4BD 18          CLC                     ;  | and this will keep
$0F/B4BE 6D 6C 10    ADC $106C  [$00:106C]   ;  | in effect
$0F/B4C1 8D 5C 10    STA $105C  [$00:105C]   ;  | until Y < $43
$0F/B4C4 C9 43       CMP #$43                ;  | 
$0F/B4C6 90 04       BCC $04    [$B4CC]      ;  | 
$0F/B4C8 CE 6C 10    DEC $106C  [$00:106C]   ; /
$0F/B4CB 60          RTS                     ;

$0F/B4CC A9 42       LDA #$42                ; \
$0F/B4CE 8D 5C 10    STA $105C  [$00:105C]   ; / fixed Y value while he's moving
$0F/B4D1 AD 60 10    LDA $1060  [$00:1060]   ;
$0F/B4D4 D0 15       BNE $15    [$B4EB]      ;
$0F/B4D6 AD 5D 10    LDA $105D  [$00:105D]   ; \  keeps going until
$0F/B4D9 18          CLC                     ;  | last 5 bits of X are 00000
$0F/B4DA 69 00       ADC #$00                ;  | this snaps him to one of:
$0F/B4DC 29 1F       AND #$1F                ;  | 00, 20, 40, 60, 80, A0, C0, E0
$0F/B4DE D0 0B       BNE $0B    [$B4EB]      ; /  
$0F/B4E0 A9 14       LDA #$14                ; \  once the state is finished
$0F/B4E2 8D 60 10    STA $1060  [$00:1060]   ;  | load $14 frames of timer
$0F/B4E5 A9 06       LDA #$06                ;  | and change state to $06
$0F/B4E7 8D 5F 10    STA $105F  [$00:105F]   ; /
$0F/B4EA 60          RTS                     ;

$0F/B4EB AD 5D 10    LDA $105D  [$00:105D]   ;
$0F/B4EE EA          NOP                     ;
$0F/B4EF EA          NOP                     ;
$0F/B4F0 EA          NOP                     ;
$0F/B4F1 29 07       AND #$07                ;
$0F/B4F3 A8          TAY                     ;
$0F/B4F4 B9 8D B4    LDA $B48D,y[$00:B48D]   ;
$0F/B4F7 8D 64 10    STA $1064  [$00:1064]   ;
$0F/B4FA B9 95 B4    LDA $B495,y[$00:B495]   ;
$0F/B4FD 8D 65 10    STA $1065  [$00:1065]   ;
$0F/B500 B9 9D B4    LDA $B49D,y[$00:B49D]   ;
$0F/B503 8D 74 10    STA $1074  [$00:1074]   ;
$0F/B506 AC 62 10    LDY $1062  [$00:1062]   ;
$0F/B509 BD 00 79    LDA $7900,x[$00:7900]   ; \
$0F/B50C C9 07       CMP #$07                ;  | if table value is 7 
$0F/B50E F0 08       BEQ $08    [$B518]      ;  | or val & gametimer == 0
$0F/B510 2D 30 00    AND $0030  [$00:0030]   ;  | move 2
$0F/B513 D0 03       BNE $03    [$B518]      ; /  else 1
$0F/B515 20 18 B5    JSR $B518  [$00:B518]   ; jumps right here, which simply performs addition twice
$0F/B518 AD 5D 10    LDA $105D  [$00:105D]   ;
$0F/B51B 18          CLC                     ;
